***corny.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a> (40947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">corn</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>; in the "hackneyed" sense, from "corn catalogue jokes", reputedly low-quality jokes that <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> formerly printed in mail-order seed catalogues.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">cornier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">corniest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Boring and unoriginal.
<dl><dd><i>The duct tape and wire <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a pretty <b><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></b> solution.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Hackneyed or excessively sentimental.
<dl><dd><i>The movie <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:okay.html>okay</a>, but the love scene <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> really <b><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></b>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>He sent a bouquet of twelve red roses and a card: "Roses are red, <a href = vnd.unilang:violet.html>Violets</a> are blue, Sugar <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sweet, And so are you." How <b><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that!</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Producing corn or grain; furnished with grains of corn.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Prior and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></b> ear.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Containing corn; tasting well of malt.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Chaucer and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>A draught of moist and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ale.html>ale</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:tipsy.html>tipsy</a>; drunk
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Forby to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">hackneyed or excessively sentimental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kitsch.html>kitsch</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">kitschy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">cheesy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tacky</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">campy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">schlocky</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">schmaltzy</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">drunk</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">drunkish</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">squiffy</span>; see Thesaurus:drunk</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cornu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:corny.html>corny</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Strong, stiff, or hard, like a horn; resembling horn.

***corolla.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:corolla.html>corolla</a> (76616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corōlla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small garland, chaplet or wreath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corōna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">garland, chaplet, wreath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:corolla.html>corolla</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">corollas</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">corollae</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">corollæ</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An outermost-but-one whorl of a flower, composed of petals, when it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not the same in appearance as the outermost whorl (the calyx); it usually comprises the petal, which may be fused.
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lawrence_Durrell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lawrence Durrell">Lawrence Durrell</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:monsieur.html>Monsieur</a></i>, Faber amp; Faber 1992, p. 125:
<dl><dd>Our <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> formed a circle like the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:corolla.html>corolla</a></b> of a flower, floating into the silence of the desert dawn with the ancient sun on our <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">corolline</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">corollate</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">corollaceous</span></li></ul>
</body>

***correctie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:correctie.html>correctie</a> (18652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">correction</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">correctio</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:corrigeren.html>corrigere</a></i> 'to correct, rectify', itself from com- (intensifying prefix, a form of con-) + <a href = vnd.unilang:regeren.html>regere</a> "to lead straight, rule" (from a Proto-Indo-European base *reg- "to move in a straight line; direct, rule, guide"): <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">correct</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:correctie.html>correctie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:correcties.html>correcties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:correctie.html>correctietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A correction, rectification</li>
<li>The action or process of correcting</li>
<li>A punishment, sanction</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A penal facility, notably a military stockade; house of correction</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>(rectification) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbetering.html>verbetering</a></span></li>
<li>(correcting) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbeteren.html>verbeteren</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:korf.html>korf</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">korver</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of ship</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vml"><a href = vnd.unilang:korf.html>korf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of ship and basket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">-ette</i>. Possibly ultimately connected to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corbita</i> (<i class="Latn mention" lang="la">navis</i>), "slow-sailing ship of burden, grain ship," which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corbis</i>.

***cotter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a> (61375)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cotters</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mechanical engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pin or wedge inserted through a <a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a> to hold machine parts together.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a> pin.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a> pin</i> are sometimes used interchangeably, although they have different functions. For a more detailed explanation see Wikipedia articles on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cotter_pin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:cotter pin"><a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a> pin</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cotter_(pin)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:cotter (pin)"><a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a> (pin)</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/split_pin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:split pin">split pin</a>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a> pin</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">cotters</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cottering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cottered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To fasten with a <a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cottage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cot</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>cotter</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cotters</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A peasant who performed labour in exchange for the right to live in a cottage.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1786</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Burns" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Burns">Robert Burns</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Cotter%27s_Saturday_Night" class="extiw" title="w:The Cotter | s Saturday Night">The <a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>Cotter</a>'s Saturday Night</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The toil-worn <a href = vnd.unilang:cotter.html>Cotter</a> frae his labour goes,— / This night his weekly moil <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> at an end,— / Collects his <a href = vnd.unilang:spades.html>spades</a>, his mattocks, and his <a href = vnd.unilang:hoes.html>hoes</a>, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">coscet</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cottager</span></li></ul>
</body>

***coven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:coven.html>coven</a> (84182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">covent</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">covent, cuvent</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">covent</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">conventum</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">conveniō</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">venio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I come</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">convent</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:coven.html>coven</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">covens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A formal group or assembly of witches.</li>
<li>A family, group or assembly of vampires.</li>
<li>A clique that shares common interests or activities.
<ul><li><b>1986</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Leavitt" class="extiw" title="w:David Leavitt">David Leavitt</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Lost_Language_of_Cranes" class="extiw" title="w:The Lost Language of Cranes">The <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a> Language of <a href = vnd.unilang:cranes.html>Cranes</a></a></i>, Penguin, paperback edition, page 12
<dl><dd>“This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a very African area”, he <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> as they maneuvered their way among the <b>covens</b> of menacing children gathered in the <a href = vnd.unilang:halls.html>halls</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">covener</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">covenstead</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">covendom</span></li></ul>
</body>

***coy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:coy.html>coy</a> (40942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kooi.html>kooi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bunk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***coyote.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:coyote.html>coyote</a> (11584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:coyote.html>coyote</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:coyote.html>coyote</a></i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nahuan_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Nahuan languages">Nahuan</a></span> language, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Nahuan" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Nahuan">Proto-Nahuan</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="azc-nah-pro">*koyootl</i>.
</p>
